One of the best Iraqi kebabs Ive tasted in a while, this place is extremely small , has a part where its a grocery store and a part where its a simple restaurant, having around 3-4 plastic tables & chairs, we didn't sit down but ordered meat kebabs for takeaway, it took a while for it to be prepared because there was only 1 person preparing the food so we waited patiently in the car for it to be prepared but damn it,it was completely worth it, the   Hot kebabs were placed in an Iraqi bread( Samon) and with added salad, onions and Sumac.

< text>
THIS. IS. THE. BEST. PLACE. EVER!

This place never disappoints.

SCRATCH THAT.

The only time this place has disappointed me is when it's been CLOSED.

My go-to meal is the chicken combo which normally comes with, shredded chicken, beans, rice, radishes, tortillas, and - if wanted - onions,  and cilantro. Lately, I've been asking for the combos just with the chicken in whole pieces with no beans and double rice. See the Plato de Pollo pic below.

By the way... I am so thankful that I will NEVER have to admit to my late grandfather that I've found a roast chicken that tastes better than his! It is so moist, tender, and flavorful!

And the rice?!?!?!?! Praise him! If I'm running errands, I'll stop in just for an 8 oz. cup - only $2, yall!

Oh, yeah! The combos come with a fountain drink, but only if you

WEAR. A. MASK!<//text>

Love this place.  Very unassuming but Wow the food and is good.

I go to El Toro Bravo for 2 different reasons and needs (yes I have food needs üòã):
1. For lunch or dinner and get usual fare: tacos, burritos, tortas etc. and they taste great.
2. Meat by the pound, cooked to perfection.

< review>
Excellent service & food!  My husband & I love these smaller Mexican restaurants & this one is our new favorite.  The cook was very accomidating to my nutritional needs (Ketogenic friendly) by creating a burrito bowl for me,  even though it's not on their menu. The carne asada was fantastic & juicy. Not dry at all. My husband got a bean & cheese burrito & was able to add yummy guacamole . He loved his burrito too. Extremely reasonably priced. I eveb have some left overs that I'm looking forward to devouring later. If I could give more stars,  I would.</review>

< Text>
In my review of the El Toro Bravo tortilleria, I gave it a "4" for the food and service but dinged it for the relatively drab location.  Enter their new restaurant a few blocks down the street, which actually has the vibrance that the other location lacks while maintaining the same commitment to service and delicious food.  I'm a hefty dude, and even I get stopped in my tracks by the food portions they offer here and often take home the rest for seconds.  If you get a combo plate (asada, pollo, or carnitas), make sure you buy a bag of chips to go with it - Just makes the experience even better.</Text>

< Review>
I just spent about 45 minutes with Wishbone Pet owner, Susanna, getting information about the kind of food that would be best suited for my 12 year old Bichon Frise, who is diabetic as well as very allergic.  I have a number of dogs and have been buying dog food for 14 years from Costco, from my vet and from Petsmart.  Never have I had such a comprehensive review of the various dog foods, both dry (grain and no-grain) and canned and dog "treats", as well as recommendations to add fiber to the diet (pumpkin has less sugar than sweet potatoes which is important in the diabetic diet).  We are now looking forward to a much healthier Bichon Frise!

Wishbone also offers a flea/tick collar by Bayer that I had not heard about--it repels fleas rather than killing the flea after the bite.  Holy smokes! that is what we need; it is the flea bite that causes so much irritation for the dogs.  The prescription pills we were giving our dogs kill the flea after it bites, we want NO bites!  And the collar works for 8 months before needing to be replaced.

I have to tell you, this is a quality operation.  I am definitely going to continue using Wishbone Pet for my pet needs.  Try them out!</Review>
< username>
Christine Kelsey< /username>

<review>I have been on this apartment for about a month now and here is what I learned.

Building - well maintained and lots of great amenity space, unfortunately closed temporarily due to the pandemic, which it should be. I like sealed concrete flooring over engineered wood and if you do find unit on 3rd floor and below. They are also better with impact noise between floors.
Management - friendly and professional. Maintenance crews provide above and beyond service which I am very thankful for. Their responsive time is prompt.
Location - 15 min walk from Downtown. Grocery market, Starbucks, dentist office and Chipotle in the building are super convenient.
Security - parking lot and all entries are controlled and I do not concern on security.
Cost - For the quality and service offered, I believe the price is very competitive.

I look forward to stay here for another year and half and definitely consider to extend my stay once my lease is over.

One recommendation to the leasing team is to hire a professional photographer to take photos of the building for advertisement. The renderings on website is not nearly as nice as the actual building.< /review><Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMRkTUTCD1nKGlNR_3Ltox0bhfzNK7Zc1QhnNoW=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNoKsyYhvmaEbqOCiwEJl2Cq3SlAR3MAOckzEn9=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</Pictures><Response>None</Response><gmapID>0x80c2c7af95c87f0d:0xe122070d552ed348</gmapID></record>

Current Resident with "REAL" Review.

On-Site Management:
- Esteban is the resident manager on site.  This guy is just AMAZING!!  He is always quick, efficient, professional and courteous.  He will go above and beyond his call of duty to ensure the residents are take care of.  Hope management sees the huge value Esteban brings to the community!!

Maintenance:
Another huge positive!  Kory is awesome!  He is detailed, knowledgeable and meticulous.  If you have an issue and he is there, he will make sure he verifies everything and resolves it before he leaves your unit.   Great asset!

Leasing:
Ruby was my leasing agent and she is another SUPERB example of outstanding service.  She is diligent and quick.  She will stay with you every step of the way until you move in.

THE BAD!!!  (Management really needs to focus this)

- AIRBNB!!  Many of the units are rented out to AIRBNB so you will see strangers constantly in/out of the building.  Feel unsafe as I run into strangers asking for access in elevators (and I have had few people get very aggressive when I refused).  I have had cars "follow" me in the garage because they do not have access keys for gate.   NEED CAMERA IN GARAGE!!

- Unruly Neighbors:   We have residents that feel "privileged " and feel they do not feel the need to follow the community rules.    We have residents throw TRASH in the trashroom floor instead of putting them in the trash shoot (not very hard)

- LOUD neighbors that like the turn up music, STOMP the floor (makes my ceiling shake) despite warnings.   For a place with "downtown" rent prices, we have quite a bit of "unclassy" neighbors.

- Security:   Night patrols and guards are work very hard. They do their best but they need more HELP!   1 person at night for both building is not an ideal security situation.  I hope management can spend the extra $$ to give us more sense of security as the surround area is not very safe.

Overall:   This place has been a good home to me so far despite the issues I am having.   My lease is coming up in a few months, Will I stay?  Not sure yet as I am hoping all the negative issues get resolved.<//review>

<user>102164723898446649980<//user><name>Cami Mccarthy< /name><time>1576617135268</time>< rating>
5< /rating>
<review>Such an iconic place for a motor enthusiast like myself!

I have heard about this place ,but this was my first time here. Located at the end or beginning of the famous snake road (whichever way you take it), it embodies the vision of a true biker pit stop!

Originally a famous stagecoach stop Vern (Veronica) bought the Rock Store in 1961 with a solid vision of the future and what she knew it would become. She transformed the property into a small town grocery store and  gas station with two retro pumps that still stand today (now non operational ,but great for photos). The property is now home to a quaint cafe and biker bar come here on the weekends to meet some of the top "who's who" in the moto world!!

The food simple ,but hits the spot. I really loved my patty melt and would recommend it to all that come. It's fast and quick with a kind staff. I want to come here for breakfast the menu looked spot on for my liking!

Both Rich and his mother Vern (the owners) were there. It happened to be her birthday-- lots attended for the special occasion and it made my first time something truly special ! Rich and his wife give tours and went out of their way walking us around and sharing with us the knowledge of the past, present, and future!

The Rock Store is a remarkable place- never before have I been to a place like this and I am looking forward to returning!!<//review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP0EL0AUj8ej0RtIjKQXCOJZ0BxABl2EVQc_fHq=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMqy5I9Nk3yG5haLYmD3bBQIIs2bMolGXCCl92K=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPdb3-g2eFkqRoKL6ZknP4VGO7I19tSxU4HaUJW=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOj01rxWsXDEC5Ry165fPUGGg_JNDQP_y-mM2Xn=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMF2sGDoEqs1laRw7uiwWpDaWbefTL9TRmAcjRD=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pictures>< Resp>

<Rating>5<//Rating><Text>I've been riding my bike here since the early 70's.  Even back then it was a biker hangout on weekends but most especially on Sundays.  Now days it still is but a whole lot bigger.
You'll see every kind of bike here on a Sunday.  From choppers, to dressers, to crotch rockets, to enduros, mopeds and even rocket propelled bikes that Jay Leno sometimes rides here on.
The canyons here are my favorite.  While I no longer drag my knees through the turns as I use to, I still enjoy cruising on them.
Please be careful and stay well inside your lane when riding here because it is a race track on Sundays and as such you'll see other riders often times drifting outside their lanes and coming right at you at a high rate of speed.   Also keep an eye behind you as you'll have others trying to pass you.  I advice you stay out of their way, and let them by.  Unless of course you're racing in which case they'd have to work their way past me.
Bottom line is I highly recommend any biker to visit this place at least once in their life.  Definitely something that should be on your bucket list.<//Text><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNnBl4KOsHiqsrAYPHbMT8Y6NyNjNK8t7PZn18_=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': <Review>I was visiting family on the West Coast in Huntington Beach and my girlfriend arranged to meet a friend in the area and arranged tour with an LA native.  We got a tour of the city and surroundings that you could never get on a bus/van.  It was a 6 hour education into an city/metropolis that even most locals won't know.  We traveled up to Malibu and had stopped at Neptune's Net but it was packed so our guide told us about this place only open from Friday through Sunday but at the end of what is called "The Snake" - AKA West Mulholland Hwy.  The food was not fancy but SOLID!  I got a bacon cheeseburger and fries.  It's a local hangout - started life as a stop on the Pony Express, then became a stagecoach stop, then a place for gas and now a place for motorcyclist to have fun after riding "The Snake" several times.  You may even meet someone like Jay Leno.  The food is SOLID - not the Cali pretense of having to have sun-dried this, or imported that.  Order, eat and be satisfied.  It's the simple pleasures that your mind latches on to for the fondest memories.  This is Mom, Baseball and American Pie stuff here.  Why is it called The Rock Shop?  The place is covered with rocks!  Go there.<//Review><gmap_id>0x80e823c0b577cae3:0xfb85751bf82a757b<//gmap_id>< Time>

<name>Andy S</name><date>1456263963781<//date>< Rating>
5</Rating>
< review>
Gathering place for gear-heads old and young.  Stop by for a little history lesson or see cutting edge motorized machinery.  After you recharge at the diner, go enjoy endless scenic canyon roads in the area.  Head to the overlook area a few miles south and watch the leaned over motorcycles, exotic supercars and cyclists navigate through a technical section of Mulholland Hwy known as "The Snake".  Stay in your lane and be courteous, you never know where and IF the LEO's are hiding.< /review>

115710363035307735701<//user>

0x80e823c0b577cae3:0xfb85751bf82a757b<//gmapID>
<pictures>None<//pictures>< Time>
1500416097564<//Time>
< Review>
I'm a motorcyclist and bicyclist, so I've been up Mulholland to and past the Rock Store more times than I can remember over the past few decades. Generally very quiet weekdays and a madhouse on weekend mornings with (dozens of) motorcycles lined up and filling the small parking area and the shoulder of the road in both directions.  The tuner "Tokyo drift" car kids and trustafarian/ middle age crisis Porche/ Lambo crowd run up and down Mulholland on weekend mornings as well but you don't see them stopping at the RS, likely due to the lack of parking.
There are non-working gas pumps outside (psych!) and a gift shop and busy coffee shop/ cafe inside, with inside and outdoor patio dining.
The cafe is the kind of place that's so busy on the weekends that the waitresses are spoiled and don't really work that hard for their tips- like a tourist trap restaurant.  Take your order, bring your food, refill your coffee, bring your check. Nothing more. They'll have a line outside regardless, and no one goes there for the service.  I tried to fill my bicycle water bottles this past weekend, the waitress inside (with easy access to water and ice) shrugged and sent me to the bartender up at the patio, who said he "has no water at his bar" [huh??] and told me I could fill my bottles in the [fairly dirty] men's room from the handwash sink.  Not much of a culture of customer service here, but it's a roadside dive, so what do you want.
4 stars I guess because of the location and vibe, not because of the place itself.</Review>
<user_name>John Anderson<//user_name>< response>
None< /response>
